367\t    // Apply vars_map (simultaneous rename).\n   368\t    if let Some(ref vm) = step.vars_map {\n   369\t        let obj = vars.as_object_mut().unwrap();\n   370\t\n   371\t        // 1. Insert all target keys (with values from snapshots).\n   384\t        for (_, target, val) in snapshots {\n   385\t            if let Some(v) = val {\n   386\t                obj.insert(target, v);\n 376\t        \"files_skipped\": agg_skipped.into_iter().collect::<Vec<_>>(),\n   377\t    })\n   378\t}\n   379\t\n   380\t// ── Workflow execution human output ──────────────────────────────\n   381\t\n   382\tpub fn format_workflow_human(\n   383\t    result: &workflow::WorkflowResult,\n   384\t    dry_run: bool,\n   385\t    verbose: bool,\n   386\t) {\n   387\t    if dry_run {\n   388\t 394\t    let mut failed = 0usize;\n   395\t\n   396\t    for (i, step) in result.steps.iter().enumerate() {\n   397\t        match step {\n   398\t            workflow::StepResult::Success { recipe,               total,\n   404\t                    recipe\n   405\t                );\n   406\t                format_human(operations, false, verbose);\n   407\t                succeeded += 1;\n   408\t            }\n   409\t            workflow::StepResult::Skipped { recipe, reason } => {\n   410\t                eprintln!(\n   411\t                    \"\\n{} {}/{}: {} {} — {}\",\n   412\t                    \"Step\".bold(),\n   413\t                    i + 1,\n   414\t                    total,\n   415\t                    \"skip\".yellow(),\n   416\t                    recipe,\n   417\t   423\t                error,\n   424\t                operations,\n   425\t                rendered_content: _,\n   426\t            } => {\n   427\t                eprintln!(\n   428\t 433\t                    recipe\n   434\t                );\n   435\t                if !operations.is_empty() {\n   436\t                    format_human(operations, false, verbose);\n   437\t                }\n   438\t                let se = error.structured_error();\n   439\t                eprintln!(\"    what: {}\", se.what);\n   440\t                eprintln!(\"    where: {}\", se.where_);\n   441\t                eprintln!(\"    why: {}\", se.why);\n   442\t                eprintln!(\"    hint: {}\", se.hint);\n   443\t                failed += 1;\n   444\t            }\n   445\t        }\n   446\t    }\n   447\t\n   448\t    eprintln!(\n   449\t        \"\\n{} steps: {} succeeded, {} skipped, {} failed\",\n   450\t        total, succeeded, skipped, failed\n   451\t    );\n It extracts only the\n   150\t/// first identifier from expressions like `{{ user.name }}` (yields \"user\", not\n   151\t/// \"user.name\"). Falls back to \"unknown\" if no match is found. minijinja does not\n   152\t/// expose the undefined variable name directly, so this is the best we can do for v0.1.\n   153\tfn find_undefined_variable(template_source: &str, error_line: Option<usize>, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   154\t    let var_keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n   155\t        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\n   156\t        None => vec![],\n   157\t    };\n   158\t\n   159\t    // Extract variable references from the template.\n   160\t    // Matches {{ name }}, {{ name | filter }}, {{ name.attr }}, etc.\n   161\t    let re = regex::Regex::new(r\"\\{\\{[\\s-]*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\").unwrap();\n   162\t    // Also check {% if/for/elif blocks\n   163\t    let block_re = regex::Regex::new(r\"\\{%[\\s-]*(?:if|elif|for\\s+\\w+\\s+in|set\\s+\\w+\\s*=)\\s+([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\").unwrap();\n   164\t\n   165\t    let lines: Vec<&str> = template_source.lines().collect();\n   166\t\n   167\t    // If we have a line number, check that line first\n   168\t    if let Some(line_num) = error_line.filter(|&l| l > 0 && l <= lines.len()) {\n   169\t        let line = lines[line_num - 1];\n   170\t        for cap in re.captures_iter(line).chain(block_re.captures_iter(line)) {\n   171\t            let name = &cap[1];\n   172\t            if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n   173\t                return name.to_string();\n   174\t            }\n   175\t        }\n   176\t    }\n   177\t\n   178\t    // Fall back to scanning the entire template\n   179\t    for cap in re.captures_iter(template_source).chain(block_re.captures_iter(template_source)) {\n   180\t        let name = &cap[1];\n   181\t        if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n   182\t            return name.to_string();\n   183\t        }\n   184\t    }\n   185\t\n   186\t    \"unknown\".to_string()\n   187\t}\n   188\t\n   189\t/// Generate a \"did you mean?\" hint using Levenshtein distance.\n   190\t/// Looks at all keys in the provided variable context.\n   191\tfn did_you_mean_hint(var_name: &str, vars: &Value) -> String {\n   192\t    let keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n   193\t        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\n   194\t        None => return format!(\"check variable name '{var_name}'\"),\n   195\t    };\n   196\t\n   197\t    if keys.is_empty() {\n   198\t        return format!(\"check variable name '{}' — no variables were provided\", var_name);\n   199\t    }\n   200\t\n   201\t    let mut best_match: Option<(&str, usize)> = None;\n   202\t    for key in &keys {\n   203\t        let dist = strsim::levenshtein(var_name, key);\n   204\t        if dist <= 3 && (best_match.is_none() || dist < best_match.unwrap().1) {\n   205\t            best_match = Some((key, dist));\n   206\t        }\n   207\t    }\n   208\t\n   209\t    match best_match {\n   210\t        Some((suggestion, _)) => format!(\"did you mean '{suggestion}'?\"),\n   211\t        None => format!(\"check variable name '{}' — available variables: {}\", var_name, keys.join(\", \")),\n   212\t    }\n   213\t}\n   214\t\n Value::String(_) => \"string\",\n   308\t        Value::Array(_) => \"array\",\n   309\t        Value::Object(_) => \"object\",\n   310\t    }\n   311\t}\n   312\t\n   313\t// ── Tests 8\t/// Execute a replace operation: find and replace a region in an existing file.\n     9\tpub fn execute(\n    10\t    rendered_path: &str,\n    11\t    rendered_content: &str,\n    12\t    spec: Run {\\n    84\\t        /// Path to the recipe YAML file\\n    85\\t        recipe: PathBuf,\\n    86\\t    },\\n    87\\t    /// Execute a multi-recipe workflow\\n    88\\t    Workflow {\\n    89\\t        /// Path to the workflow YAML file\\n    90\\t        path: PathBuf,\\n    91\\t    },\\n    92\\t}\\n    93\\t\\n    94\\tfn main() {\\n    95\\t    let cli = Cli::parse();\\n    96\\t    let   Commands::Validate { recipe } => cmd_validate(&recipe, cli.json),\\n   109\\t        Commands::Vars { recipe } => cmd_vars(&recipe),\\n   110\\t        Commands::Render { template, to } => {\\n   111\\t            cmd_render(&template, to.as_deref(), cli.vars.as_deref(), cli.vars_file.as_deref(), cli.vars_stdin)\\n   112\\t        }\\n   113\\t        Commands::Run { recipe } => {\\n   114\\t            cmd_run(\\n   115\\t                &recipe,\\n   116\\t                cli.vars.as_deref(),\\n   117\\t                cli.vars_file.as_deref(),\\n   118\\t cli.base_dir.as_deref(),\\n   124\\t                cli.verbose,\\n   125\\t            )\\n   126\\t        }\\n   127\\t        Commands::Workflow { path } => {\\n   128\\t            cmd_workflow(\\n   129\\t                &path,\\n   130\\t                cli.vars.as_deref(),\\n   131\\t                cli.vars_file.as_deref(),\\n   132\\t                cli.vars_stdin,\\n   133\\t                cli.dry_run,\\n   134\\t                cli.json,\\n   135\\t                cli.quiet,\\n   136\\t                cli.force,\\n   137\\t                cli.base_dir.as_deref(),\\n   138\\t                cli.verbose,\\n   139\\t            )\\n   140\\t        }\\n   141\\t    }\\n   142\\t}\\n   143\\t\\n   144\\tfn cmd_validate(path: &std::path::Path, json: bool) -> Result<i32, JigError> {\\n   145\\t    match workflow::detect_file_type(path)? {\\n   146\\t        workflow::FileType::Recipe => {\\n   147\\t            let recipe = Recipe::load(path)?;\\n   148\\t            if json {\\n   149\\t                let output = build_validate_json(&recipe);\\n   150\\t                println!(\\\"{}\\\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\\n   151\\t            } else {\\n   152\\t                eprintln!(\\\"Recipe is valid: {}\\\", path.display());\\n   153\\t                eprintln!(\\\"  Variables: {}\\\", recipe.variables.len());\\n   154\\t                if !recipe.variables.is_empty() {\\n   155\\t                    for name in recipe.variables.keys() {\\n   156\\t                        eprintln!(\\\"    - {name}\\\");\\n   157\\t                    }\\n   158\\t                }\\n   159\\t                let op_types = summarize_op_types(&recipe);\\n   160\\t                eprintln!(\\\"  Operations: {} ({})\\\", recipe.files.len(), op_types);\\n   161\\t            }\\n   162\\t        }\\n   163\\t        workflow::FileType::Workflow => {\\n 167\\t                println!(\\\"{}\\\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&output).unwrap());\\n   168\\t            } else {\\n   169\\t                eprintln!(\\\"Workflow is valid: {}\\\", path.display());\\n   170\\t                if let Some(ref name) = validation.name {\\n   171\\t                    eprintln!(\\\"  Name: {name}\\\");\\n   172\\t                }\\n   173\\t                eprintln!(\\\"  Variables: {}\\\", validation.variables.len());\\n   174\\t                if !validation.variables.is_empty() {\\n   175\\t                    for name in validation.variables.keys() {\\n   176\\t                        eprintln!(\\\"    - {name}\\\");\\n   177\\t                    }\\n   178\\t                }\\n   179\\t                let unconditional = validation.steps.iter().filter(|s| !s.conditional).count();\\n   180\\t                let conditional = validation.steps.iter().filter(|s| s.conditional).count();\\n   181\\t                eprintln!(\\n   182\\t                    \\\"  Steps: {} ({} unconditional, {} conditional)\\\",\\n   183\\t                    validation.steps.len(),\\n   184\\t                    unconditional,\\n   185\\t                    conditional\\n   186\\t                );\\n   187\\t                for (i, step) in validation.steps.iter().enumerate() {\\n   188\\t                    let cond = if step.conditional { \\\" (conditional)\\\" } else { \\\"\\\" };\\n   189\\t                    let status = if step.valid { \\\"valid\\\" } else { \\\"INVALID\\\" };\\n   190\\t                    eprintln!(\\\"    {}. {} — {}{}\\\", i + 1, step.recipe, status, cond);\\n   191\\t                }\\n   192\\t            }\\n   193\\t        }\\n   194\\t    }\\n   195\\t\\n   196\\t    Ok(0)\\n   197\\t}\\n   198\\t\\n   199\\tfn cmd_vars(path: &std::path::Path) -> Result<i32, JigError> {\\n   200\\t    let vars = match workflow::detect_file_type(path)? {\\n   201\\t        workflow::FileType::Recipe => {\\n   202\\t            let recipe = Recipe::load(path)?;\\n   203\\t            variables::vars_json(&recipe.variables)\\n   204\\t        }\\n   205\\t        workflow::FileType::Workflow => {\\n   206\\t            let wf = workflow::load_workflow(path)?;\\n   207\\t            variables::vars_json(&wf.variables)\\n   208\\t        }\\n   209\\t    };\\n   210\\t    println!(\\\"{}\\\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&vars).unwrap());\\n   211\\t    Ok(0)\\n   212\\t}\\n   213\\t\\n   214\\tfn cmd_render(\\n   215\\t    template_path: &std::path::Path,\\n   216\\t    to: Option<&std::path::Path>,\\n   217\\t    inline_vars: Option<&str>,\\n   218\\t    vars_file: Option<&std::path::Path>,\\n   219\\t    vars_stdin: bool,\\n   220\\t) -> Result<i32, JigError> {\\n   221\\t    // Read the template file\\n   222\\t    let source = std::fs::read_to_string(template_path).map_err(|e| {\\n   223\\t        JigError::TemplateRendering(crate::error::StructuredError {\\n   224\\t            what: format!(\\\"cannot read template file '{}'\\\", template_path.display()),\\n   225\\t            where_: template_path.display().to_string(),\\n   226\\t            why: e.to_string(),\\n   227\\t            hint: \\\"check the template file path\\\".into(),\\n   228\\t        })\\n   229\\t    })?;\\n   230\\t\\n   231\\t    // Collect variables from all sources (no recipe context → no type validation)\\n   232\\t    let vars = variables::collect_vars(inline_vars, vars_file, vars_stdin)?;\\n   233\\t\\n   234\\t    // Create standalone environment and render\\n   235\\t    let env = renderer::create_standalone_env();\\n   236\\t    let source_name = template_path.display().to_string();\\n   237\\t    let output = renderer::render_string(&env, &source, &vars, &source_name)?;\\n   238\\t\\n   239\\t    // Write to file or stdout\\n   240\\t    match to {\\n   241\\t        Some(path) => {\\n   242\\t            if let Some(parent) = path.parent().filter(|p| !p.as_os_str().is_empty()) {\\n   243\\t                std::fs::create_dir_all(parent).map_err(|e| {\\n   244\\t                    JigError::FileOperation(crate::error::StructuredError {\\n   245\\t                        what: format!(\\\"cannot create output directory '{}'\\\", parent.display()),\\n   246\\t                        where_: path.display().to_string(),\\n   247\\t                        why: e.to_string(),\\n   248\\t                        hint: \\\"check directory permissions\\\".into(),\\n   249\\t                    })\\n   250\\t                })?;\\n   251\\t            }\\n   252\\t            std::fs::write(path, &output).map_err(|e| {\\n   253\\t                JigError::FileOperation(crate::error::StructuredError {\\n   254\\t                    what: format!(\\\"cannot write output file '{}'\\\", path.display()),\\n   255\\t                    where_: path.display().to_string(),\\n   256\\t                    why: e.to_string(),\\n   257\\t                    hint: \\\"check file permissions\\\".into(),\\n   258\\t                })\\n   259\\t            })?;\\n   260\\t        }\\n   261\\t        None => {\\n   262\\t            print!(\\\"{output}\\\");\\n   263\\t        }\\n   264\\t    }\\n   265\\t\\n   266\\t    Ok(0)\\n   267\\t}\\n   268\\t\\n   269\\t#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]\\n   270\\tfn cmd_run(\\n   271\\t    recipe_path: &std::path::Path,\\n   272\\t    inline_vars: Option<&str>,\\n   273\\t    vars_file: Option<&std::path::Path>,\\n   274\\t    vars_stdin: bool,\\n   275\\t    dry_run: bool,\\n   276\\t    force_json: bool,\\n   277\\t    quiet: bool,\\n   278\\t    force: bool,\\n   279\\t    base_dir: Option<&std::path::Path>,\\n   280\\t    verbose: bool,\\n   281\\t) -> Result<i32, JigError> {\\n   282\\t    let mode = output::detect_mode(force_json);\\n   283\\t\\n   284\\t    // Helper: handle pre-operation errors respecting --json and --quiet.\\n   285\\t    // In JSON/piped mode, emit a JSON error envelope to stdout.\\n   286\\t    // In human mode with --quiet, suppress stderr.\\n   287\\t    // Returns Ok(exit_code) so main() doesn't double-print.\\n   288\\t    let handle_early_error = |e: JigError| -> Result<i32, JigError> {\\n   289\\t        let code = 300\\t                        \\\"why\\\": se.why,\\n   301\\t                        \\\"hint\\\": se.hint,\\n   302\\t                        \\\"rendered_content\\\": \\\"\\\",\\n   303\\t                    }],\\n   304\\t                    \\\"files_written\\\": [],\\n   305\\t                    \\\"files_skipped\\\": [],\\n   306\\t                });\\n   307\\t                println!(\\\"{}\\\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&json).unwrap());\\n   308\\t                Ok(code)\\n   309\\t            }\\n   310\\t            output::OutputMode::Human => {\\n   311\\t                if !quiet {\\n   312\\t                    eprintln!(\\\"{e}\\\");\\n   313\\t                }\\n   314\\t                Ok(code)\\n   315\\t            }\\n   316\\t        }\\n   317\\t    };\\n   318\\t\\n   319\\t    // 1. Load and validate recipe (exit 1 on failure).\\n   320\\t    let recipe = match Recipe::load(recipe_path) {\\n\",\"exit_code\":0,\"status\":\"completed\"}}\n    13\t{\"type\":\"item.started\",\"item\":{\"id\":\"item_5\",\"type\":\"command_execution\",\"command\":\"/bin/zsh -lc \\\"nl -ba src/workflow.rs | sed -n '261,620p'\\\"\",\"aggregated_output\":\"\",\"exit_code\":null,\"status\":\"in_progress\"}}\n    14\t{\"type\":\"item.completed\",\"item\":{\"id\":\"item_5\",\"type\":\"command_execution\",\"command\":\"/bin/zsh -lc \\\"nl -ba src/workflow.rs | sed -n '261,620p'\\\"\",\"aggregated_output\":\"   261\\t        }\\n   262\\t    }\\n   263\\t\\n   264\\t    // Resolve recipe paths and validate.\\n   265\\t    let mut steps = Vec::with_capacity(raw.steps.len());\\n   266\\t    let mut      if !resolved.exists() {\\n   271\\t            validation_errors.push((i, raw_step.recipe.clone(), StructuredError {\\n   272\\t                what: format!(\\\"recipe file not found: '{}'\\\", raw_step.recipe),\\n   273\\t                where_: format!(\\\"steps[{}].recipe\\\", i),\\n   274\\t                why: format!(\\\"resolved path '{}' does not exist\\\", resolved.display()),\\n   275\\t                hint: \\\"check the recipe path — it is resolved relative to the workflow file's directory\\\".into(),\\n   276\\t            }));\\n   277\\t        } else {\\n   278\\t            // Validate the recipe is structurally valid.\\n   279\\t            match Recipe::load(&resolved) {\\n   280\\t                Ok(_) => {}\\n   281\\t                Err(e) => {\\n   282\\t !validation_errors.is_empty() {\\n   304\\t        // Return first error (with step context).\\n   305\\t        let (_, _, err) = validation_errors.into_iter().next().unwrap();\\n   306\\t        return Err(JigError::RecipeValidation(err));\\n   307\\t    }\\n   308\\t\\n   309\\t    Ok(Workflow {\\n   310\\t        name: raw.name,\\n   311\\t        description: raw.description,\\n   312\\t Workflow validation (for jig validate) ───────────────────────\\n   320\\t\\n   321\\tpub struct WorkflowValidation {\\n   322\\t    pub name: Option<String>,\\n   323\\t    pub description: Option<String>,\\n   324\\t    pub variables: IndexMap<String, VariableDecl>,\\n   325\\t    pub steps: Vec<StepValidation>,\\n   326\\t}\\n   327\\t\\n   328\\tpub struct StepValidation {\\n   329\\t    pub recipe: String,\\n   330\\t    pub valid: bool,\\n   331\\t    pub conditional: bool,\\n   332\\t    pub when: Option<String>,\\n   333\\t    pub error: Option<String>,\\n   334\\t}\\n   335\\t\\n   336\\tpub fn validate_workflow(path: &Path) -> Result<WorkflowValidation, JigError> {\\n   337\\t    let workflow = load_workflow(path)?;\\n   338\\t\\n   339\\t    let steps = workflow\\n   340\\t        .steps\\n   341\\t        .iter()\\n   342\\t        .map(|step| StepValidation {\\n   343\\t            recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   344\\t            valid: true, // already validated in load_workflow\\n   345\\t            conditional: step.when.is_some(),\\n   346\\t            when: step.when.clone(),\\n   347\\t            error: None,\\n   348\\t        })\\n workflow.variables,\\n   355\\t        steps,\\n   356\\t    })\\n   357\\t}\\n   358\\t\\n   359\\t// ── Variable resolution ──────────────────────────────────────────\\n   360\\t\\n   361\\tpub fn resolve_step_variables(\\n   362\\t    workflow_vars: &Value,\\n   363\\t    step: &WorkflowStep,\\n   364\\t) -> Result<Value, JigError> {\\n   365\\t    let mut vars = workflow_vars.clone();\\n   366\\t\\n   367\\t    // Apply vars_map (simultaneous rename).\\n   368\\t    if let Some(ref vm) = step.vars_map {\\n   369\\t        let obj = vars.as_object_mut().unwrap();\\n   370\\t\\n   371\\t        // 1. Snapshot all source values.\\n   372\\t        let mut snapshots: Vec<(String, String, Option<Value>)> = Vec::new();\\n   373\\t        for (source, target) in vm {\\n   374\\t            let val = obj.get(source).cloned();\\n   375\\t            snapshots.push((source.clone(), target.clone(), val));\\n   376\\t        }\\n   377\\t\\n   378\\t        // 2. Remove all source keys.\\n   379\\t        for (source, _, _) in &snapshots {\\n   380\\t            obj.remove(source);\\n   381\\t        }\\n   382\\t\\n   383\\t        // 3. Insert all target keys (with values from snapshots).\\n   384\\t        for (_, target, val) in snapshots {\\n   385\\t            if let Some(v) = val {\\n   386\\t                obj.insert(target, v);\\n   387\\t            }\\n   388\\t            // AC-4.7: nonexistent source → silently ignored\\n   389\\t        }\\n   390\\t    }\\n   391\\t\\n   392\\t    // Apply vars overrides.\\n   393\\t    if let Some(ref overrides) = step.vars {\\n   394\\t        let obj = vars.as_object_mut().unwrap();\\n   395\\t        for (key, val) in overrides {\\n   396\\t            obj.insert(key.clone(), val.clone());\\n   397\\t        }\\n   398\\t    }\\n   399\\t\\n   400\\t    Ok(vars)\\n   401\\t}\\n   402\\t\\n   403\\t// ── When evaluation ──────────────────────────────────────────────\\n   404\\t\\n   405\\tpub fn evaluate_when(when_expr: &str, vars: &Value) -> Result<bool, JigError> {\\n   406\\t    let env = renderer::create_standalone_env();\\n   407\\t    let rendered = renderer::render_string(&env, when_expr, vars, \\\"when\\\")?;\\n   408\\t    let trimmed = rendered.trim();\\n   409\\t\\n   410\\t    // Falsy: empty, \\\"false\\\" (case-insensitive), \\\"0\\\"\\n   411\\t    if trimmed.is_empty() || trimmed.eq_ignore_ascii_case(\\\"false\\\") || trimmed == \\\"0\\\" {\\n   412\\t        Ok(false)\\n   413\\t    } else {\\n   414\\t        Ok(true)\\n   415\\t    }\\n   416\\t}\\n   417\\t\\n   418\\t// ── Workflow execution ───────────────────────────────────────────\\n   419\\t\\n   420\\tpub fn execute_workflow(\\n   421\\t    workflow: &Workflow,\\n   422\\t    vars: Value,\\n   423\\t    ctx: &mut ExecutionContext,\\n   424\\t    verbose: bool,\\n   425\\t) -> WorkflowResult {\\n   426\\t    let mut step_results = Vec::with_capacity(workflow.steps.len());\\n   427\\t\\n   428\\t    for (i, step) in workflow.steps.iter().enumerate() {\\n   429\\t        // (a) Evaluate when condition against workflow-level vars.\\n   430\\t        if let Some(ref when_expr) = step.when {\\n   431\\t            match evaluate_when(when_expr, &vars) {\\n   432\\t                Ok(true) => {} // proceed\\n   433\\t                Ok(false) => {\\n   434\\t                    step_results.push(StepResult::Skipped {\\n   435\\t                        recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   436\\t                        reason: \\\"when condition evaluated to false\\\".into(),\\n   437\\t                    });\\n   438\\t                    continue;\\n   439\\t                }\\n   440\\t                Err(e) => {\\n   441\\t                    let effective_mode = step.on_error.unwrap_or(workflow.on_error);\\n   442\\t                    step_results.push(StepResult::Error {\\n   443\\t                        recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   444\\t                        error: e,\\n   445\\t                        operations: vec![],\\n   446\\t                        rendered_content: None,\\n   447\\t                    });\\n   448\\t                    match effective_mode {\\n   449\\t                        OnError::Stop => break,\\n   450\\t                        OnError::Continue | OnError::Report => continue,\\n   451\\t                    }\\n   452\\t                }\\n   453\\t            }\\n   454\\t        }\\n   455\\t\\n   456\\t        // (b) Resolve step variables.\\n   457\\t        let step_vars = match resolve_step_variables(&vars, step) {\\n   458\\t            Ok(v) => v,\\n   459\\t            Err(e) => {\\n   460\\t                let effective_mode = step.on_error.unwrap_or(workflow.on_error);\\n   461\\t                step_results.push(StepResult::Error {\\n   462\\t                    recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   463\\t                    error: e,\\n   464\\t                    operations: vec![],\\n   465\\t                    rendered_content: None,\\n   466\\t                });\\n   467\\t                match effective_mode {\\n   468\\t                    OnError::Stop => break,\\n   469\\t                    OnError::Continue | OnError::Report => continue,\\n   470\\t                }\\n   471\\t            }\\n   472\\t        };\\n   473\\t\\n   474\\t        // (c) Load recipe.\\n   475\\t        let recipe = match Recipe::load(&step.resolved_recipe) {\\n   476\\t            Ok(r) => r,\\n   477\\t            Err(e) => {\\n   478\\t                let effective_mode = step.on_error.unwrap_or(workflow.on_error);\\n   479\\t                step_results.push(StepResult::Error {\\n   480\\t                    recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   481\\t                    error: e,\\n   482\\t                    operations: vec![],\\n   483\\t                    rendered_content: None,\\n   484\\t                });\\n   485\\t                match effective_mode {\\n   486\\t                    OnError::Stop => break,\\n   487\\t                    OnError::Continue | OnError::Report => continue,\\n   488\\t                }\\n   489\\t            }\\n   490\\t        };\\n   491\\t\\n   492\\t        // (d) Validate step vars against recipe declarations.\\n   493\\t        let validated_vars = match variables::validate_variables(&recipe.variables, &step_vars) {\\n   494\\t            Ok(v) => v,\\n   495\\t            Err(e) => {\\n   496\\t                let effective_mode = step.on_error.unwrap_or(workflow.on_error);\\n   497\\t                step_results.push(StepResult::Error {\\n   498\\t                    recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   499\\t                    error: e,\\n   500\\t                    operations: vec![],\\n   501\\t                    rendered_content: None,\\n   502\\t                });\\n   503\\t                match effective_mode {\\n   504\\t                    OnError::Stop => break,\\n   505\\t                    OnError::Continue | OnError::Report => continue,\\n   506\\t                }\\n   507\\t            }\\n   508\\t        };\\n   509\\t\\n   510\\t        // (e) Execute recipe via partial_results)) => {\\n   519\\t                let rendered = extract_rendered_from_error(&e);\\n   520\\t                let effective_mode = step.on_error.unwrap_or(workflow.on_error);\\n   521\\t                step_results.push(StepResult::Error {\\n   522\\t                    recipe: step.recipe.clone(),\\n   523\\t                    error: e,\\n   524\\t                    operations: partial_results,\\n   525\\t                    rendered_content: rendered,\\n   526\\t                });\\n   527\\t                match effective_mode {\\n   528\\t                    OnError::Stop => break,\\n   529\\t                    OnError::Continue | OnError::Report => {\\n   530\\t                        // Record step index for error reporting\\n   531\\t                        let _ = i; // used for context in output formatting\\n   532\\t                        continue;\\n   533\\t                    }\\n   534\\t                }\\n   535\\t            }\\n   536\\t        }\\n   537\\t    }\\n   538\\t\\n   539\\t    WorkflowResult {\\n   540\\t        name: workflow.name.clone(),\\n   541\\t        on_error: workflow.on_error,\\n   542\\t        steps: step_results,\\n   543\\t    }\\n   544\\t}\\n   545\\t\\n   546\\t// ── run_recipe (extracted from cmd_run logic) ────────────────────\\n   547\\t\\n   548\\t/// Execute a loaded recipe with provided 0\\n   615\\t    }\\n   616\\t}\\n   617\\t\\n   618\\tfn build_validate_json(recipe: &Recipe) -> serde_json::Value {\\n   619\\t    let vars = variables::vars_json(&recipe.variables);\\n   620\\t\\n     recipe::FileOp::Replace { .. } => replace_count += 1,\\n   660\\t            recipe::FileOp::Patch { .. } => patch_count += 1,\\n   661\\t        }\\n   662\\t    }\\n   663\\t    let mut parts = \\\"none\\\".to_string()\\n   678\\t    } else {\\n   679\\t        parts.join(\\\", \\\")\\n   680\\t    }\\n   681\\t}\\n   682\\t\\n   683\\t#[cfg(test)]\\n   684\\tmod tests {\\n   685\\t    use minijinja::ErrorKind::UndefinedError => {\\n   100\\t            // minijinja doesn't include the variable name in the error.\\n   101\\t            // Extract it from the template source by finding 104\\t\\n   105\\t            JigError::TemplateRendering(StructuredError {\\n   106\\t                what: format!(\\\"undefined variable '{}'\\\", var_name),\\n   107\\t                where_: 145\\t\\n   146\\t/// Find the undefined variable in a template by scanning for references\\n   147\\t/// not present in the variable context.\\n   148\\t///\\n   149\\t/// Limitation: this is a best-effort heuristic using regex. It extracts only the\\n   150\\t/// first identifier from expressions like `{{ user.name }}` (yields \\\"user\\\", not\\n   151\\t/// \\\"user.name\\\"). Falls back to \\\"unknown\\\" if no match is found. minijinja does not\\n   152\\t/// expose the undefined variable name directly, so this is the best we can do for v0.1.\\n   153\\tfn find_undefined_variable(template_source: &str, error_line: Option<usize>, vars: &Value) -> String {\\n   154\\t    let var_keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\\n   155\\t        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\\n   156\\t        None => vec![],\\n   157\\t    };\\n   158\\t\\n   159\\t    // Extract variable references from the template.\\n   160\\t    // Matches {{ name }}, {{ name | filter }}, {{ name.attr }}, etc.\\n   161\\t    let re = regex::Regex::new(r\\\"\\\\{\\\\{[\\\\s-]*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\\\").unwrap();\\n   162\\t    // Also check {% if/for/elif blocks\\n   163\\t    let block_re = regex::Regex::new(r\\\"\\\\{%[\\\\s-]*(?:if|elif|for\\\\s+\\\\w+\\\\s+in|set\\\\s+\\\\w+\\\\s*=)\\\\s+([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\\\").unwrap();\\n   164\\t\\n   165\\t    let lines: Vec<&str> = template_source.lines().collect();\\n   166\\t\\n   167\\t    // If we have a line number, check that line first\\n   168\\t    if let Some(line_num) = error_line.filter(|&l| l > 0 && l <= lines.len()) {\\n   169\\t        let line = lines[line_num - 1];\\n   170\\t        for cap in re.captures_iter(line).chain(block_re.captures_iter(line)) {\\n   171\\t            let name = &cap[1];\\n   172\\t            if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\\n   173\\t                return name.to_string();\\n   174\\t            }\\n   175\\t        }\\n   176\\t    }\\n   177\\t\\n   178\\t    // Fall back to scanning the entire template\\n   179\\t    for cap in re.captures_iter(template_source).chain(block_re.captures_iter(template_source)) {\\n   180\\t        let name = &cap[1];\\n   181\\t        if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\\n   182\\t            return name.to_string();\\n   183\\t        }\\n   184\\t    }\\n   185\\t\\n   186\\t    \\\"unknown\\\".to_string()\\n   187\\t}\\n   188\\t\\n   189\\t/// Generate a \\\"did you mean?\\\" hint using Levenshtein distance.\\n   190\\t/// Looks at all keys in the provided variable context.\\n   191\\tfn did_you_mean_hint(var_name: &str, vars: &Value) -> String {\\n   192\\t    let keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\\n   193\\t        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\\n   194\\t        None => return format!(\\\"check variable name '{var_name}'\\\"),\\n   195\\t    };\\n   196\\t\\n   197\\t    if keys.is_empty() {\\n   198\\t        return format!(\\\"check variable name '{}' — no variables were provided\\\", var_name);\\n   199\\t    }\\n   200\\t\\n   201\\t    let mut best_match: Option<(&str, usize)> = None;\\n   202\\t    for key in &keys {\\n   203\\t        let dist = strsim::levenshtein(var_name, key);\\n   204\\t        if dist <= 3 && (best_match.is_none() || dist < best_match.unwrap().1) {\\n   205\\t            best_match = Some((key, dist));\\n   206\\t        }\\n   207\\t    }\\n   208\\t\\n   209\\t    match best_match {\\n   210\\t        Some((suggestion, _)) => format!(\\\"did you mean '{suggestion}'?\\\"),\\n   211\\t        None => format!(\\\"check variable name '{}' — available variables: {}\\\", var_name, keys.join(\\\", \\\")),\\n   212\\t    }\\n   213\\t}\\n   214\\t\\n file: Option<&Path>,\\n   111\\t    stdin: bool,\\n   112\\t) -> Result<Value, JigError> {\\n   113\\t    let file_val = match file {\\n   114\\t        Some(path) => Some(parse_vars_file(path)?),\\n   115\\t        None => None,\\n   116\\t    };\\n   117\\t    let stdin_val = if stdin {\\n   118\\t        Some(parse_vars_stdin()?)\\n   119\\t    } else {\\n   120\\t        None\\n   121\\t    };\\n   122\\t    let inline_val = match inline {\\n   123\\t        Some(s) => Some(parse_vars_inline(s)?),\\n   124\\t        None => None,\\n   125\\t    };\\n   126\\t\\n   127\\t    let mut Ok(merged)\\n   138\\t}\\n   139\\t\\n   140\\t// ── Public API: validation ─────────────────────────────────────────\\n   141\\t\\n   142\\t/// Validate and merge variables against recipe in declarations pass through without error (AC-2.12).\\n   146\\t#[allow(dead_code)] // Used in later phases (jig run) and tests\\n   147\\tpub fn validate_variables(\\n   148\\t    decls: &IndexMap<String, VariableDecl>,\\n   149\\t    provided: &Value,\\n   150\\t) -> Result<Value, JigError> {\\n   151\\t    let provided_obj = provided.as_object().cloned().unwrap_or_default();\\n   152\\t\\n   153\\t    // Start with defaults, then overlay provided values.\\n   154\\t    let mut merged = serde_json::Map::new();\\n   155\\t    for (name, decl) in decls {\\n   156\\t        if let 161\\t        merged.insert(key.clone(), val.clone());\\n   162\\t    }\\n   163\\t\\n   164\\t    let mut errors = Vec::new();\\n   165\\t\\n   166\\t    for (name, decl) in decls {\\n   167\\t variable '{name}'\\\"),\\n   171\\t                    where_: format!(\\\"variable '{name}'\\\"),\\n   172\\t                    why: format!(\\\"variable '{name}' is declared as required but no value was provided\\\"),\\n   173\\t                    hint: format!(\\\"add '{name}' to --vars, e.g. --vars '{{\\\\\\\"{}\\\\\\\":...}}'\\\", name),\\n   174\\t                });\\n   175\\t            }\\n   176\\t            None => {\\n   177\\t                // Not required, no default — just absent. 183\\t    }\\n   184\\t\\n   185\\t    if !errors.is_empty() {\\n   186\\t        return Err(JigError::VariableValidation(errors));\\n   187\\t    }\\n   188\\t\\n   189\\t    Ok(Value::Object(merged))\\n   190\\t}\\n   191\\t\\n   192\\t// ── Internal helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────\\n   193\\t\\n   194\\tfn merge_json(base: &mut Value, overlay: &Value) {\\n   195\\t    if let (Some(base_obj), Some(overlay_obj)) = (base.as_object_mut(), overlay.as_object()) {\\n   196\\t        for (key, val) in overlay_obj {\\n   197\\t            base_obj.insert(key.clone(), val.clone());\\n   198\\t        }\\n   199\\t    }\\n   200\\t}\\n   201\\t\\n   202\\tfn check_type(name: &str, decl: &VariableDecl, val: &Value, errors: &mut !val.is_string() {\\n   208\\t                errors.push(type_mismatch_error(name, \\\"string\\\", actual_type, val));\\n   209\\t            }\\n   210\\t        }\\n   211\\t        VarType::Number => {\\n   212\\t            if !val.is_number() {\\n   213\\t                errors.push(type_mismatch_error(name, \\\"number\\\", actual_type, val));\\n   214\\t            }\\n   215\\t        }\\n   216\\t        VarType::Boolean => {\\n   217\\t            if !val.is_boolean() {\\n   218\\t                errors.push(type_mismatch_error(name, \\\"boolean\\\", actual_type, val));\\n   219\\t            }\\n   220\\t        }\\n   221\\t        VarType::Array => {\\n   222\\t            if !val.is_array() {\\n   223\\t                errors.push(type_mismatch_error(name, \\\"array\\\", actual_type, val));\\n   224\\t            } else if let Some(ref item_type) = decl.items {\\n   225\\t                check_array_items(name, item_type, val.as_array().unwrap(), errors);\\n   226\\t + rendered_content.len() + 1);\\n    89\\t            result.push_str(&file_content);\\n    90\\t            if !file_content.ends_with('\\\\n') && !file_content.is_empty() {\\n    91\\t ctx.virtual_files.insert(target.clone(), new_content);\\n   116\\t    }\\n   117\\t\\n   118\\t    OpResult::Success {\\n   119\\t        action: \\\"inject\\\",\\n   120\\t        path: target,\\n   121\\t        lines: injected_lines,\\n   122\\t        location: Some(location),\\n   123\\t        rendered_content: content_for_verbose,\\n   124\\t        scope_diagnostics: None,\\n   125\\t    }\\n   126\\t}\\n   127\\t\\n   128\\t/// Inject content after or before a regex match.\\n   129\\t/// Returns (new_content, location_description) or an OpResult::Error.\\n   130\\t#[allow(clippy::result_large_err)]\\n   131\\tfn inject_after_before(\\n   132\\t    file_content: &str,\\n   133\\t    rendered_content: &str,\\n   134\\t    pattern: &str,\\n   135\\t    at: &MatchPosition,\\n   136\\t    is_after: bool,\\n   137\\t    target: &std::path::Path,\\n   138\\t) -> Result<(String, String), OpResult> {\\n   139\\t    let re = Regex::new(pattern).expect(\\\"regex was validated at parse time\\\");\\n   140\\t\\n   141\\t    let lines: Vec<&str> = file_content.lines().collect();\\n   142\\t    let matching_indices: Vec<usize> = lines\\n   143\\t        .iter()\\n   144\\t        .enumerate()\\n   145\\t        .filter(|(_, line)| re.is_match(line))\\n   146\\t        .map(|(i, _)| i)\\n   147\\t        .collect();\\n   148\\t\\n   149\\t    if matching_indices.is_empty() {\\n   150\\t        return Err(OpResult::Error {\\n   151\\t            path: target.to_path_buf(),\\n   152\\t            error: StructuredError {\\n   153\\t                what: format!(\\\"regex pattern matched no lines in '{}'\\\", target.display()),\\n   154\\t                where_: target.display().to_string(),\\n   155\\t                why: format!(\\\"pattern '{}' did not match any line in the file\\\", pattern),\\n   156\\t                hint: \\\"check the regex pattern against the file contents\\\".into(),\\n   157\\t            },\\n   158\\t            rendered_content: rendered_content.to_string(),\\n   159\\t        });\\n   160\\t    }\\n   161\\t\\n   162\\t    let match_idx = match at {\\n   163\\t        MatchPosition::First => matching_indices[0],\\n   164\\t        MatchPosition::Last => *matching_indices.last().unwrap(),\\n   165\\t    };\\n   166\\t\\n   167\\t    // Build new content by inserting at the right position.\\n   168\\t    let direction = if is_after { \\\"after\\\" } else { \\\"before\\\" };\\n   169\\t    let at_str = match at {\\n   170\\t        MatchPosition::First => \\\"first\\\",\\n   171\\t        MatchPosition::Last => \\\"last\\\",\\n   172\\t    };\\n   173\\t    // Line numbers are 1-based for human display.\\n   174\\t    let location = format!(\\\"{direction}:{pattern} ({at_str} match, line {})\\\", match_idx + 1);\\n   175\\t\\n   176\\t    let mut result = String::new();\\n   177\\t    let has_trailing_newline = file_content.ends_with('\\\\n');\\n   178\\t\\n   179\\t    if is_after {\\n   180\\t        // Insert after match_idx line.\\n   181\\t        for (i, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {\\n   182\\t            result.push_str(line);\\n   183\\t            result.push('\\\\n');\\n   184\\t            if i == match_idx {\\n   185\\t                result.push_str(rendered_content);\\n   186\\t                if !rendered_content.ends_with('\\\\n') {\\n   187\\t                    result.push('\\\\n');\\n   188\\t                }\\n   189\\t            }\\n   190\\t        }\\n   191\\t    } else {\\n   192\\t        // Insert before match_idx line.\\n   193\\t        for (i, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {\\n   194\\t            if i == match_idx {\\n   195\\t                result.push_str(rendered_content);\\n   196\\t                if !rendered_content.ends_with('\\\\n') {\\n   197\\t                    result.push('\\\\n');\\n   198\\t                }\\n   199\\t            }\\n   200\\t            result.push_str(line);\\n   201\\t            result.push('\\\\n');\\n   202\\t        }\\n   203\\t    }\\n   204\\t\\n   205\\t    // Preserve original trailing newline behavior.\\n   206\\t    if !has_trailing_newline && result.ends_with('\\\\n') {\\n   207\\t        result.pop();\\n   208\\t    }\\n   209\\t\\n   210\\t    Ok((result, location))\\n
